shared_focus = {
	id = CVA_increase_industrial_mobilisation
	icon = GFX_goal_Focus_Military_Mobilisation
	x = 3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = CVA_stick_to_the_plan
	cost = 5.00
	prerequisite = { 
	    focus = CVA_stick_to_the_plan 
	}
	bypass = {
	    has_country_flag = CVA_finished_the_revolution
		OR = {
		    has_idea = war_economy
			has_idea = tot_economic_mobilisation
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus CVA_plantations_for_the_people"
		one_random_arms_factory = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
			    has_idea = civilian_economy 
			}
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = civilian_economy
				add_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
			    has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation 
			}
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
				add_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
			    has_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation

			}
		}

			}
			swap_ideas = {

			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe_1
				variant_name = "Early Fighter"
				amount = 100
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
			has_tech = early_fighter
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = fighter_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 2
				category = light_fighter
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe
				amount = 100
				producer = CVA
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_technology = {
				early_fighter = 1
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = fighter_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				category = light_fighter
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe
				amount = 100
				producer = CVA
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { 
	    FOCUS_FILTER_AIRFORCE_BONUS
		FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH
	}
}
